                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   *   **Patent:** Right to an invention (e.g., manufacturing method). Duration: 20 years from application date. Not applicable if publicly known/used before filing.
*   **Trademark:** Right to a mark identifying one's goods/services.
    *   **Mark:** Symbols, letters, figures, sounds, smells, holograms, movements, or colors. Trade names can also be registered.
    *   **Service Mark:** Trademark for services (e.g., academies). Website domains can be registered as service marks (a registered service mark takes precedence over a registered domain).
    *   Duration: Can be used virtually permanently by renewing every 10 years.
*   **Design:** Right to the aesthetic form, shape, color, or composition of an article or font. Duration: 20 years from registration date.
*   **Utility Model:** Right to protect practical designs, typically for improving the shape and structure of existing products to enhance practicality. Lower technical level than patents. Duration: 10 years from application date.

**Acquisition of IPR:**
*   Acquired by **registering with the Korean Intellectual Property Office**.
*   **First-to-file rule** applies.
*   Protection is **country-specific**: rights are recognized only in the country where registration is made; separate applications are needed in each country for international protection.
*   **Purpose:** Grant exclusive rights for a certain period to the creator, promoting technological and industrial development, after which anyone can use it.

**Violations of Industrial Property Rights:**
These involve misleading the public about the registration status of products or services.

*   **False Patent Claims:**
    *   Displaying an unregistered/non-existent patent number.
    *   Marking a product as patented when the application isn't complete.
    *   Using marks easily confused with patent marks.
    *   Marking a utility model, design, or trademark as a patent.
*   **False Trademark Claims:**
    *   Displaying an unregistered mark as if it were a registered or applied-for trademark.
    *   Using false trademarks in commercial materials (ads, signboards, packaging).
    *   Theft of renowned domestic and foreign trademarks.
*   **False Utility Model/Design Claims:**
    *   Marking an item as a utility model/design registration/application when it's not registered or pending.
    *   Displaying marks likely to be confused with registered utility models or designs.

**Punishment for False Display of IPR:**
*   Imprisonment for up to 3 years or a fine of up to 20 million won.
*   This is an **offense not subject to complaint**, meaning a third party (not just the victim) can file criminal charges.

---

## 3. New Intellectual Property Rights

**Definition:** These rights protect emerging areas like computer programs, biotechnology, semiconductor designs, and digital content, which are difficult to protect with traditional IPRs (like patents and copyrights).

**Types of New Intellectual Property Rights:**

*   **Industrial Copyright:** Computer programs, artificial intelligence, databases.
*   **High-Tech Industrial Property Rights:** Semiconductor integrated circuit layout design, biotechnology.
*   **Information Property Rights:** Trade secrets, multimedia.

**WTO Scope:** The World Trade Organization (WTO) broadly includes these new rights within its definition of intellectual property, covering all rights from intellectual activities in industry, science, literature, or art.

---

## 4. Unfair Competition Prevention & Trade Secret Protection

### A) Unfair Competition Prevention

**Concept:** Aims to prevent unfair business practices, such as misusing well-known trademarks/trade names and infringing on trade secrets.

**Acts of Unfair Competition include:**

*   **Misusing Well-Known Marks:** Using identical or similar names, trade names, trademarks, or product packaging of another widely known person/company in Korea.
*   **False Origin/Quality Marks:** Making false claims about the origin, quality, content, manufacturing process, usage, or quantity of goods in advertising or on products.
*   **Agent/Representative Misuse of Trademarks:** Using a trademark registered in another country (by Paris Convention/WTO members) without good cause by an agent or former agent.
*   **Domain Name Squatting:** Registering, holding, transferring, or using a domain name identical or similar to another's well-known name/trademark without legitimate right, for purposes like selling it, preventing legitimate use, or gaining commercial profit.
*   **Copying Product Shapes:** Transferring, lending, exhibiting, importing, or exporting goods whose shape has been copied from another's manufactured goods.
*   **Misusing Business Ideas/Information:** Unfairly using another person's technical or business ideas (with economic value) obtained during negotiations (e.g., business proposals, auctions) for one's own or a third party's business interests, or providing such information to others to exploit.

### B) Trade Secret Protection

**Concept of a Trade Secret:** Information (like production methods, sales methods, technical/business information) that is:
1.  **Not publicly known:** The information is a secret.
2.  **Has independent economic value:** It's useful for business activities and has financial worth.
3.  **Managed as a secret:** Efforts have been made to keep it confidential (e.g., confidentiality notices, access restrictions, confidentiality agreements). *Information accessible to anyone is not a trade secret.*

**Acts Constituting Infringement of Trade Secrets:**

*   **Improper Acquisition & Use/Disclosure:** Acquiring trade secrets through theft, deception, coercion, or other improper means, then using or disclosing them.
*   **Knowledgeable Use/Disclosure:** Using or disclosing trade secrets after acquiring them, knowing they were improperly obtained, or without such knowledge due to gross negligence.
*   **Breach of Confidentiality:** Using or disclosing trade secrets to gain improper benefits or harm the owner while under a contractual or other duty to maintain secrecy.

**Precedents for Infringement of Trade Secrets:**
*   Adding only new features based on another's source code.
*   Developing and selling substantially similar programs by performing **reverse analysis** (reverse engineering) of program code, especially if it violates a contract or technical protection measures.

**Precedents that are NOT Infringement of Trade Secrets:**
*   When the programming language and implementation method of software are completely different.
*   Performing reverse analysis of legally purchased program code to obtain information necessary for compatibility, *when such information cannot be easily obtained otherwise* (Article 101-4 of Copyright Act).

---

## Pages 217-221


Here is a simplified, easy-to-read learning guide based on the provided text (Pages 217-221).

---

## IT Business & Ethics: Learning Guide (Pages 217-221)

### 1. Unfair Competition & Intellectual Property

This section outlines various acts considered unfair competition, with a focus on trade secrets.

#### 1.1 Acts of Unfair Competition

Specific acts are defined as unfair competition, protecting various forms of intellectual property:

*   **Trademark Infringement by Agents/Representatives:**
    *   An agent/representative of a trademark owner (or someone who was within 1 year) uses an identical or similar trademark.
    *   The trademark must be registered in countries party to the Paris Convention, WTO, or Trademark Law Treaty.
    *   This includes selling, distributing, exporting, or importing goods with such a trademark.
*   **Domain Name Misuse (Cybersquatting):**
    *   Registering, holding, transferring, or using a domain name identical or similar to another person's name, trade name, or widely known trademark in South Korea.
    *   Done without a legitimate right and for specific purposes:
        *   Selling or lending the mark (e.g., trademark) to the legitimate owner or a third party.
        *   Preventing the legitimate owner from registering or using the domain name.
        *   Obtaining other commercial profits.
*   **Copying Product Shapes:**
    *   Transferring, lending, exhibiting, importing, or exporting goods whose shape has been copied from another person's manufactured goods.
*   **Unfair Use of Technical/Business Ideas:**
    *   Unfairly using information containing another person’s technical or business ideas with economic value.
    *   Information was obtained during negotiations or transactions (e.g., business proposal, auction, public offering).
    *   Used for personal or third-party business interests, violating the original purpose of the information's provision.
    *   Also includes providing such information to another person for their advantage.

#### 1.2 Trade Secrets

A crucial aspect of business protection.

*   **Concept of a Trade Secret:**
    *   Information (e.g., production methods, sales methods, technical/business info).
    *   **Requirements:**
        1.  **Non-publicity:** Not publicly known.
        2.  **Economic Usefulness:** Useful for business activities and has independent economic value.
        3.  **Confidentiality:** Managed as a secret through reasonable efforts (e.g., non-disclosure agreements, access restrictions). Information known to everyone is not a trade secret.

*   **Infringement of Trade Secrets:**
    *   **Acquisition & Use:** Acquiring trade secrets by theft, deception, coercion, or other improper means, then using or disclosing them.
    *   **Knowledge of Improper Acquisition:** Using or disclosing trade secrets after acquiring them, knowing (or being grossly negligent about the fact) that they were improperly obtained.
    *   **Breach of Duty:** Using or disclosing trade secrets for improper benefits or to harm the owner, while under a contractual or other duty to maintain secrecy.

*   **Legal Precedents for Trade Secret Infringement:**
    *   **Examples of Infringement:**
        *   Adding only new features based on existing (protected) source code.
        *   Developing, producing, and selling substantially similar programs by reverse engineering (violates Copyright Act Article 101-4).
        *   Reverse analysis conducted in violation of a contract, especially when technical protection measures were in place to prevent it.
    *   **Examples NOT Constituting Infringement:**
        *   Software developed with a completely different programming language and implementation method.
        *   Reverse analysis of a legally purchased program to obtain information necessary for compatibility, when that information cannot be easily obtained otherwise (Copyright Act Article 101-4).

### 2. Ethical Challenges in the IT Industry

The rapid advancement of IT brings new ethical considerations.

#### 2.1 Overview

*   **Trends:** The IT industry revolution fuels new products and services through technology convergence.
*   **Issues:** Despite improved technical competence, a lack of ethical awareness leads to increasing side effects like safety accidents, information leakage, and privacy invasion.
*   **Impact:** These issues hinder IT business development.
*   **Solution:** It's crucial to examine ethical issues in all service fields and cultivate strong ethical awareness to ensure sustainable IT development.

#### 2.2 Learning Objectives

*   Explain ethical issues related to the latest IT business services.
*   Describe ethical compliance within these services.

#### 2.3 Key Ethical Areas

*   Cloud Computing Ethics
*   Autonomous Vehicle Ethics
*   Big Data Ethics Issues
*   Artificial Intelligence Ethics
*   Drone Ethics

#### 2.4 The Autonomous Vehicle Dilemma (Case Study)

A practical example of an ethical challenge in emerging technology.

*   **Scenario (The Trolley Problem applied to AI):**
    *   An autonomous car's brakes fail.
    *   Option 1: Drive straight, hit 5 pedestrians.
    *   Option 2: Swerve, hit 1 pedestrian.
    *   **Additional Complexity:** If the 1 person hit by swerving is an occupant of the car, who should the vehicle save?
*   **Survey Results (2016, Science journal):**
    *   **Public Opinion:** 78% of people said it's more ethical to save the most pedestrians.
    *   **Personal Choice Dilemma:** When asked if they would buy a car that prioritizes pedestrian safety over their own (as an occupant), most answered no.
*   **Core Challenge:** This highlights an inevitable ethical dilemma in the Fourth Industrial Revolution. We must understand technology's benefits and potential problems from misuse to ensure safe use.

### 3. Major Ethical Issues in Latest IT Business Services

#### 3.1 Artificial Intelligence (AI) Ethics

The rise of AI and intelligent robots has made AI ethics a central concern.

*   **Context:** Intelligent robots and AI-powered products/services are driving the 4th Industrial Revolution, creating an intelligent information society.
*   **Scope of AI Ethics:**
    *   **Moral & Philosophical Ethics:** Pertains to the identity of AI/robots and their relationship with humans.
    *   **Practical Ethics:** Required for professionals involved in developing and using AI that is distributed to consumers.

*   **Key Global Initiatives & Principles for AI Ethics:**
    *   **2010 UK EPSRC "Principles of Robots":** Focused on AI issues from the perspective of designers, builders, and users.
    *   **Oct 2016 US NSTC "Preparing for the Future of Artificial Intelligence":** Emphasized the state's role in developing AI as an economic engine and building social consensus on future AI issues.
    *   **Dec 2016 IEEE "Ethically Aligned Design":** Stressed designing AI and automatic systems with ethical aspects in mind from the start. Addressed accountability, transparency, privacy, and employment issues.
    *   **Dec 2016 Japanese Ministry of Internal Affairs and Communications "Proposal of Discussion toward Formulation of AI R&D Guideline":** Presented eight core principles for AI developers (e.g., transparency, user support, controllability, security, safety, privacy protection, ethics, accountability).
    *   **Jan 2017 US FLI "Asilomar AI Principles":** Signed by over 2,000 AI scholars, futurists, and industry experts (including Stephen Hawking, Elon Musk). It outlined 23 principles for AI development, focusing on safety, transparency, accountability, privacy, profit sharing, and preventing an AI arms race.
    *   **Feb 2017 European Union (EU) "Civil Law Rules on Robotics":** Advised all involved in robot development to prioritize human dignity, respect personal privacy, and put human safety first in planning, design, and implementation.

## Pages 220-224


Here is a simplified, easy-to-read learning guide based on the provided text:

---

## Learning Guide: IT Business & Ethics - Focus on AI

### 1. Introduction: The Ethical Dilemma of Autonomous Technology

*   **Problem:** New technologies, like Artificial Intelligence (AI) and Autonomous Vehicles (AVs), create complex ethical dilemmas.
*   **Example (Autonomous Vehicle):**
    *   **Scenario:** A self-driving car with broken brakes faces a choice:
        *   Hit 5 pedestrians (driving straight).
        *   Hit 1 pedestrian (turning).
        *   Hit 1 car occupant (turning, if the injured person isn't a pedestrian).
    *   **Survey Results (2016 Science Journal):**
        *   **Ethical Preference:** 78% of people said it's more ethical to save the most lives (5 pedestrians).
        *   **Purchase Intent:** However, most people *would not buy* an AV that prioritizes pedestrian safety over the car occupant's (who could be them or their family).
    *   **Conclusion:** This highlights a fundamental dilemma: what is rational/ethical for society vs. what is desired for personal safety.
*   **Key Takeaway:** Understanding the ethical issues of new technology is crucial for its safe and beneficial use, considering both its advantages and potential misuse.

### 2. Major Ethical Issues of Artificial Intelligence (AI)

*   **Context:** The rise of intelligent robots and products marks the 4th Industrial Revolution and an intelligent information society.
*   **Two Main Types of AI Ethical Issues:**
    1.  **Moral & Philosophical Ethics:** Pertains to the identity of AI/robots and their relationship with humans.
    2.  **Practical Ethics:** Required from professionals (developers, users) involved in creating and distributing AI.

#### Key International AI Ethics Initiatives & Principles:

Several organizations have issued guidelines for AI ethics:

*   **2010 - UK EPSRC (Engineering & Physical Sciences Research Council):** Presented "Principles of Robots," covering AI issues from the perspective of designers, builders, and users.
*   **2016 (Oct) - US NSTC (National Science and Technology Commission):** Published "Preparing for the future of artificial intelligence." Emphasized:
    *   AI as an economic growth engine.
    *   Need for national/social consensus on future AI issues.
*   **2016 (Dec) - IEEE (Institute of Electrical and Electronics Engineers):** Announced "Ethically Aligned Design." Focused on:
    *   Designing AI with ethical aspects from the start.
    *   Accountability of suppliers, transparency, awareness, privacy, employment.
*   **2016 (Dec) - Japan's Ministry of Internal Affairs and Communications:** Proposed "Discussion toward Formulation of AI R&D Guideline." Presented eight principles for AI developers: transparency, user support, controllability, security, safety, personal info protection, ethics, accountability.
*   **2017 (Jan) - US FLI (Future of Life Institute):** Announced "Asilomar AI Principles."
    *   23 principles for AI development, signed by over 2,000 experts.
    *   Keywords: safety, transparency, accountability, privacy protection, shared profits, avoiding AI arms race.
*   **2017 (Feb) - EU (European Union):** Released "Civil Law Rules on Robotics." Advised developers, researchers, and designers to prioritize:
    *   Human dignity, personal privacy, and human safety when planning, designing, and implementing robots.

#### Ethical Guidelines for AI Developers:

*   **Reason for Specific Guidelines:** AI's performance is affected by human interaction, its behavior is difficult to predict, and it's more complex/less secure than conventional software.
*   **Developer Responsibilities:**
    1.  Design & develop AI accurately, clearly, fairly, and faithfully to client orders.
    2.  Conduct quality certification and supply AI to business operators.
    3.  Maintain product responsibility and provide continuous upgrades.
    4.  Prepare and provide malfunction countermeasures within the product.
    5.  Comply with global standard design/implementation and share knowledge.
    6.  Act honestly and unbiasedly with customers, obey laws (societal, national, global), and respect intellectual property (universal social responsibility).

### 3. Foundational AI Ethics: Asimov's Three Laws of Robotics

*   **Origin:** Introduced by Isaac Asimov in his 1942 short story "Runaround" and formalized in the 1950 collection "I, Robot."
*   **Purpose:** These are "commands" embedded *within* an AI robot at manufacturing, forming a "moral code" for the AI itself, not ethical rules for developers. They regulate robot behavior and define their relationship with humans.
*   **The Three Laws (in order of precedence):**
    1.  **First Law:** A robot may not injure a human being or, through inaction, allow a human being to come to harm.
    2.  **Second Law:** A robot must obey the orders given it by human beings except where such orders would conflict with the First Law.
    3.  **Third Law:** A robot must protect its own existence as long as such protection does not conflict with the First or Second Law.
*   **Later Addition (1984):** A "Zeroth Law" was later implied/added: "A robot may not harm humanity, or, by inaction, allow humanity to come to harm." (This supersedes all three original laws).

### 4. Advanced AI Ethics: The Asilomar AI Principles

*   **Origin:** Published by the Future of Life Institute (FLI) in the U.S.
*   **Structure:** Divided into three main categories:
    *   **Research Issues (Items 1-5):** Focus on the direction and conduct of AI research.
    *   **Ethics and Values (Items 6-18):** Address the moral implications and desired characteristics of AI systems.
    *   **Longer-term Issues (Items 19-23):** Consider the societal impact and future challenges of advanced AI.

#### Key Asilomar AI Principles Summarized:

*   **Research Issues:**
    *   **Research Goal:** Create *beneficial* intelligence, not just undirected intelligence.
    *   **Research Funding:** Fund research to ensure AI's beneficial use.
    *   **Science-Policy Link:** Foster healthy exchange between AI researchers and policymakers.
    *   **Research Culture:** Encourage cooperation, trust, and transparency among AI developers.
    *   **Race Avoidance:** Teams should cooperate to avoid compromising safety standards for speed.

*   **Ethics and Values:**
    *   **Safety:** AI systems must be safe, secure, and verifiably so throughout their operation.
    *   **Failure Transparency:** If AI causes harm, the reason must be ascertainable.
    *   **Judicial Transparency:** Autonomous systems in judicial decisions need auditable explanations.
    *   **Responsibility:** Designers/builders are accountable for the moral implications of their AI's use/misuse.
    *   **Value Alignment:** AI goals and behaviors must align with human values throughout operation.
    *   **Human Values:** AI systems should respect human dignity, rights, freedoms, and cultural diversity.
    *   **Personal Privacy:** People should control their data, given AI's analytical power.
    *   **Liberty and Privacy:** AI's use of personal data must not unreasonably restrict people's liberty.
    *   **Shared Benefit:** AI technologies should benefit and empower as many people as possible.
    *   **Shared Prosperity:** Economic prosperity from AI should be broadly shared.
    *   **Human Control:** Humans should choose if and how to delegate decisions to AI, to achieve human-chosen objectives.
    *   **Non-subversion:** Control of advanced AI should improve, not undermine, societal and civic processes.

*   **Longer-term Issues:**
    *   **AI Arms Race:** Avoid an arms race in lethal autonomous weapons.

---

## Pages 223-227


Here is a simplified, easy-to-read learning guide based on the provided text:

---

## IT Business and Ethics Learning Guide

### 1. Foundational Ethical Principles in IT

For IT developers and businesses, key ethical considerations include:

*   **Design & Development:**
    *   Accuracy, clarity, fairness, faithfulness to business needs.
    *   Refuse bribery.
    *   Ensure fair assessment, equitable treatment.
*   **Quality & Supply:**
    *   Conduct quality certification.
    *   Ensure product safety, health, and welfare.
*   **Maintenance & Upgrades:**
    *   Maintain responsibility for products.
    *   Provide continuous upgrades.
    *   Fair use of materials.
*   **Malfunction Countermeasures:**
    *   Develop and provide solutions against malfunctions.
    *   Ensure safety, health, welfare.
*   **Global Standards & Knowledge Sharing:**
    *   Comply with global technology standards.
    *   Enhance understanding and share knowledge.
    *   Consider operational conditions, legal compliance.
*   **Universal Social Responsibility:**
    *   Integrity, discretion, respect for property rights.
    *   Refuse bribery in public speech.
    *   Nonmaleficence (doing no harm).
    *   Contribute to the field of expertise.
    *   Cooperation, eco-friendliness.

### 2. Asimov's Three Laws of Robotics

These foundational principles, introduced by Isaac Asimov, are **moral codes embedded within AI robots at the manufacturing stage**, not ethics for AI developers. They dictate a robot's behavior:

*   **First Law:** A robot may not injure a human being or, through inaction, allow a human being to come to harm.
*   **Second Law:** A robot must obey orders given by humans, *unless* those orders conflict with the First Law. (First Law takes precedence).
*   **Third Law:** A robot must protect its own existence, *unless* such protection conflicts with the First or Second Law. (First and Second Laws take precedence).

**Later Addition (1984):** "A robot may not harm humanity, or, by inaction, allow humanity to come to harm." (Often referred to as the "Zeroth Law," preceding the others).

### 3. The Asilomar AI Principles (by Future of Life Institute - FLI)

These principles are divided into three categories:

#### A. Research Issues
1.  **Research Goal:** Create *beneficial* intelligence, not just undirected intelligence.
2.  **Research Funding:** Investments in AI should include funding for safety research.
3.  **Science-Policy Link:** Foster healthy exchange between AI researchers and policymakers.
4.  **Research Culture:** Promote cooperation, trust, and transparency among AI developers.
5.  **Race Avoidance:** Teams developing AI should cooperate to avoid compromising safety standards.

#### B. Ethics and Values
1.  **Safety:** AI systems must be safe and secure throughout their operational life, verifiably so.
2.  **Failure Transparency:** If an AI causes harm, it must be possible to ascertain why.
3.  **Judicial Transparency:** Autonomous systems in judicial decisions need auditable explanations for humans.
4.  **Responsibility:** Designers/builders of advanced AI are responsible for its moral implications (use, misuse, actions).
5.  **Value Alignment:** Highly autonomous AI must be designed so its goals and behaviors align with human values.
6.  **Human Values:** AI systems should be compatible with human dignity, rights, freedoms, and cultural diversity.
7.  **Personal Privacy:** People should control the data they generate, especially given AI's analytical power.
8.  **Liberty and Privacy:** AI use of personal data must not unreasonably restrict people's liberty.
9.  **Shared Benefit:** AI technologies should benefit and empower as many people as possible.
10. **Shared Prosperity:** Economic prosperity from AI should be broadly shared across humanity.
11. **Human Control:** Humans should choose how and whether to delegate decisions to AI.
12. **Non-subversion:** AI power should improve, not undermine, social and civic processes.
13. **AI Arms Race:** An arms race in lethal autonomous weapons must be avoided.

#### C. Longer-Term Issues
1.  **Capability Caution:** Avoid strong assumptions about future AI capabilities, as no consensus exists.
2.  **Importance:** Advanced AI is a profound change; plan for and manage it with commensurate care.
3.  **Risks:** Catastrophic or existential AI risks require significant planning and mitigation efforts.
4.  **Recursive Self-Improvement:** AI designed for self-improvement/replication needs strict safety and control.
5.  **Common Good:** Superintelligence should be developed for widely shared ethical ideals and the benefit of *all humanity*, not just one entity.

### 4. Ethical Issues of Big Data

Big data, while a core of industrial growth, can create harmful data if not managed ethically. It requires ethical operation throughout its lifecycle: collection, management, use, and disposal.

#### Key Ethical Concerns:
*   **Abuse Prevention:** Ensure ethical operation and prevent misuse of big data systems.
*   **Data Security:** Implement access control, safe storage, anonymization/encryption, prevent privacy infringement, and ensure safe data destruction.
*   **Sensitive Information:** Restrict creation of big data on sensitive individual information (ideologies, beliefs, political opinions).
*   **Purpose Limitation:** Prohibit using analyzed information for purposes other than intended; prevent unauthorized use.
*   **Personal Information:** Prevent misuse and leakage of personal information.
*   **Ownership & Rights:** Establish policies on big data ownership and rights.
*   **Commercial vs. Public Good:** Address the balance of using big data for commercial profit versus public benefit (e.g., health equality, medical systems).

#### Cloudera's Four Key Principles for Ethical Data Use:
1.  **Adjust Expectations:** Align expectations between organizations and individuals on data usage.
2.  **Best Practices:** Establish strong data management best practices.
3.  **Set Boundaries:** Clearly define limitations on data use.
4.  **Supervision & Regulation:** Government, industry, or self-regulation is needed.

#### Guidelines for De-identification of Personal Data:
This ensures personal data safety when utilized in big data.
1.  **Preliminary Review:** Verify if data is personal data. Non-personal data can be used freely.
2.  **De-identification:** Apply measures (delete/replace elements) to make individuals unidentifiable. Remove attributes unrelated to data use purpose.
3.  **Adequacy Assessment:** A panel assesses if de-identified data can be easily re-identified by combining it with other data.
4.  **Follow-up Management:** Implement safety measures and monitor for re-identification during use.
    *   **Managerial Safety:** Designate a person-in-charge, prohibit data sharing, destroy data after use.
    *   **Technical Safety:** Restrict access, manage access records, install security programs.
    *   **Leakage Protection:** Analyze cause, implement further safety measures, withdraw/destroy leaked data.

### 5. Ethical Issues of Autonomous Vehicles (Self-Driving Cars)

Autonomous vehicles offer stability, convenience, and efficiency by reducing accident rates. However, they introduce significant ethical challenges:

*   **Ethical Dilemma in Accidents:** Controversy over how to handle unavoidable accidents and determine fault/responsibility.
*   **Safety Issues:** Ensuring adequate reaction to pedestrians and obstacles; occupant protection.
*   **Hacking Risks:** Remote control attacks and system availability threats due to hacking.
*   **Life and Property Loss:** Potential for life and property loss from hacking incidents.
*   **Privacy Invasion:** Leakage of personal information (travel routes, address) collected by in-vehicle sensors.
*   **Abuse as Surveillance:** Potential for vehicles to be misused as unmanned monitoring devices, invading privacy.

### 6. Ethical Issues Related to Drones

Drones are increasingly used for hobbies, filming, and industrial purposes (delivery, monitoring, agriculture), offering real-time command, surveillance, and high-definition recording. This widespread use brings ethical concerns:

*   **Physical Accidents:** Increased crashes, collisions with buildings, and flying in restricted zones.
*   **Hacking:** Disruption of remote control, theft of captured imagery/data (e.g., combat drone data, intelligence footage).
*   **Privacy Invasion:** Illegal filming, collection, and transmission of videos related to personal life.

**Crucial Point:** Before operating drones, understanding drone-related regulations and ethical guidelines is essential.

## Pages 226-230


Here is a simplified, easy-to-read learning guide based on the provided text:

---

## IT Business and Ethics: Learning Guide

This guide covers key ethical considerations and practical guidelines for Big Data De-identification, Autonomous Vehicles, Drones, the Trolley Dilemma, and Cloud Computing.

---

### 1. Data De-identification for Big Data Utilization

**Purpose:** To enable the safe use of personal data for big data analysis by making individuals unidentifiable, while ensuring legal compliance and security.

**Procedure for De-identification:**

1.  **Preliminary Review:**
    *   **Action:** Verify if data is personal data.
    *   **Outcome:** If *not* personal data, it can be used freely.

2.  **De-identification:**
    *   **Action:** Apply measures to make individuals unidentifiable (e.g., delete or replace identifying elements from the dataset).
    *   **Principle:** Delete attributes unrelated to the data's intended use.

3.  **Adequacy Assessment:**
    *   **Action:** A "De-identification Adequacy Assessment Panel" evaluates if the de-identified data can still be easily linked back to an individual using other data.

4.  **Follow-up Management:**
    *   **Action:** Implement safety measures and monitor for potential re-identification.

**Safety Measures for De-identified Data:**

*   **Managerial:**
    *   Designate a person in charge.
    *   Prohibit sharing of de-identification data.
    *   Destroy data once its purpose is fulfilled.
*   **Technical:**
    *   Restrict access to files.
    *   Manage access records.
    *   Install and operate security programs.

**Protective Measures (if de-identified data is leaked):**

*   Analyze the cause of leakage.
*   Implement both managerial and technical safety measures to prevent more leaks.
*   Withdraw and destroy leaked data.

---

### 2. Ethical Issues of Autonomous Vehicles (Self-Driving Cars)

Autonomous vehicles (AVs) integrate sensors, communication tech, and advanced algorithms to optimize routes and improve safety. However, they introduce several ethical challenges.

**Key Ethical Issues:**

*   **Ethical Dilemma:** How to program AVs to make decisions in unavoidable accident scenarios (e.g., who to protect – occupants or pedestrians).
*   **Safety Issues:**
    *   Reliable detection and reaction to pedestrians and obstacles.
    *   Occupant protection during incidents.
*   **Hacking & Cyber Threats:**
    *   Remote control attacks by hackers.
    *   Information leakage due to malicious software.
    *   Threat of property loss or danger to life from hacking.
*   **Privacy Invasion:**
    *   Leakage of personal information (travel routes, addresses) collected by in-vehicle sensors.
    *   Potential for AVs to be misused as surveillance tools.

---

### 3. Ethical Issues Related to Drones

Drones are increasingly used in industries (delivery, monitoring) and for leisure. Their widespread use brings a rise in accidents and ethical concerns.

**Common Accidents & Concerns:**

*   Crashes, collisions with buildings, flying in no-fly zones.
*   Hacking (e.g., disrupting remote control, stealing imagery).
*   Privacy invasion (illegal filming of private life, collection of personal location data).
*   Potential for malicious use (weapons, terrorism, spy cameras).

**Ethical Guidelines for Drone Use:**

*   **Accident Prevention:** Minimize collision risks and damage.
*   **Hacking Prevention & Security:** Ensure drones have security functions to prevent information leaks and interference.
*   **Prohibition of Malicious Use:** Do not use drones as weapons, for terrorism, or as "spy cameras."
*   **Prevention of Privacy Invasion:** Do not arbitrarily collect/transmit information about others' public or private lives. Prohibit filming to identify individuals without consent or collecting personal location data.
*   **Prevention of Theft:** Secure drones to prevent data leakage if stolen.
*   **Policy Understanding & Compliance:** Know and follow drone policies specific to each country/region.
*   **Operation & Safety Education:** Receive training on drone control, safety, and accident response.

**Global Drone Operation Policies (Examples):**

| Classification | Key Drone Operation Policy Points                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| :------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| **South Korea**  | *   Daylight-only flights. <br/> *   Max altitude: 150m. <br/> *   Prohibition of dropping objects. <br/> *   Weight limit: 25kg (55 lbs).                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| **US**           | *   Daylight-only flights, within sight. <br/> *   Max altitude: 152m (500 ft). <br/> *   Max speed: 100 mph (87 knots). <br/> *   Minimum pilot age: 16 years.                                                                                                                                                                |
| **EU**           | *   No unified regulation, varies by member state. <br/> *   Mandatory electronic registration for all drones (from 2019). <br/> *   Region-wide weight limit: 136kg (330 lbs). <br/> *   **France:** Rules based on location/purpose, 25kg weight threshold. <br/> *   **Germany:** 25kg limit, public disclosure of drone photos prohibited. <br/> *   **Austria:** Drone images of identifiable individuals prohibited. |
| **Southeast Asia** | *   **General:** Strong regulation for privacy, safety, military info; pre-registration common. <br/> *   **Thailand:** Within sight, max 90m altitude, daytime only. Drones over 2kg need permission. <br/> *   **Philippines:** Daytime only. Drones over 7kg need permission. <br/> *   **Vietnam:** Extremely stringent, requires Ministry of Defense approval. |

---

### 4. The Trolley Dilemma

**Concept:** A thought experiment in ethics (by Philippa Foot) that explores moral choices in situations where sacrificing one person might save many others. It's often used to discuss programming ethics for autonomous systems.

**How it relates to Tech:**

*   **Combat Drones:** Soldiers operating drones might distance themselves from the ethical implications of lethal actions by claiming they just followed orders, avoiding the dilemma of direct responsibility.
*   **Autonomous Vehicles:** In an unavoidable accident, an AV must "choose" between different harmful outcomes (e.g., saving the driver vs. saving multiple pedestrians). Programming an AV means deciding which lives take priority.

---

### 5. Ethical Issues of Cloud Computing

Cloud service providers have responsibilities regarding user data protection and service delivery.

**Guidance for Cloud Computing Service Providers:**

*   **User Information Protection:** Strive to protect user data and provide reliable services.
*   **Quality & Performance:** Continuously improve service quality, performance, and information protection.
*   **Incident Notification:** Promptly notify users of data leaks, service interruptions, or infringement accidents.
*   **Third-Party Sharing/Other Uses:** If providing user info to a third party or using it for non-service purposes, inform the user and obtain explicit consent.
*   **Contract Termination:** Upon contract termination, return user information and destroy all possessed copies.
*   **Business Closure:** Notify users of business closure, return user information before closure, and destroy all possessed copies.

**Privacy Policy for Cloud Computing Service Providers:**

*   **Transparency:** Clearly disclose server location, applicable privacy laws, and data processing policies to customers.
*   **Access Control:** Implement robust access control functions.
*   **Regular Audits:** Periodically verify privacy policy implementation via a trusted third party and share results with customers.
*   **Justified Access:** If accessing customer data (beyond random access), provide clear reasons.
*   **Internal Management:** Establish and implement internal plans and an organization for protecting personal and customer data.
*   **Data Integrity:** Prevent unauthorized use, alteration, or damage of customer data.
*   **Complete Deletion:** Fully delete customer data when they opt out of the service.
*   **Dispute Resolution:** Provide contact information and procedures for personal data disputes.
*   **Damage Relief:** Promptly address and relieve damage in case of a personal data dispute.
